    • 暴击射击造成三倍伤害：
      • Mk1: 112,5 → 337,5（马力）;
      • Mk2: 132,35 → 397,05（hp）；
      • Mk3: 148,89 → 446,67（hp）；
      • Mk4: 165,44 → 496,32 (hp);
      • Mk5: 175,36 → 526,08（马力）;
      • Mk6: 185,29 → 555,87（马力）;
      • Mk7: 198,53 → 595,59 (hp);
      • Mk7+: 225 → 675（马力）。
    • 冰风暴的«震动冻结»装备改造将伤害减少15%而不是30%。
  • 火箭炮的«导弹发射器“轴”»装备改造:
    • 火箭的炮弹重装时间增加了20%而不是15%;
    • 齐射炮弹重装时间增加被移除；
    • 在齐射中火箭数量没有减少，现在是4个而不是3个；
    • 齐射发射火箭之间的延迟增加，变为0.5秒而不是0.25秒。
  • 过速装置:
    • 蜂王的过速装置不允许玩家在增压效果持续期间（7秒）从战斗行动中获得过速装置充能点；
    • 修复了在某些装备改造装备时，维京的过速装置伤害计算方式。
    • 极速炮在维京的过速装置激活时造成5倍伤害，而不是3倍。
  • 更新了某些货币的商店价格。


7月16日（更新655）

  • 夏季运动会活动和新的«军备竞赛»游戏模式已经在游戏中！
  • 新增了滑膛炮的«磁性颗粒»装备改造，弹夹中的最后一发子弹将禁用击中红队的激活道具。
  • 为«开发者VS玩家»活动添加了迷彩。
  • 镭射炮的变化
    • 暴击伤害现在是之前的两倍：
      • Mk1: 355 马力 → 710 马力；
      • Mk2: 437,35 马力 → 874,7 马力;
      • Mk3: 468,24 马力 → 936,48 马力;
      • Mk4: 509,41 马力 → 1018,82 马力；
      • Mk5: 560,88 马力 → 1121,76 马力；
      • Mk6: 591,76 马力 → 1183,52 马力；
      • Mk7: 622,65 马力 → 1245,3 马力；
      • Mk7+: 705 马力 → 1410 马力。
    • 狙击手模式下完全能量充能所需时间从4秒减少到3秒；
    • «重型电容器» 装备改造让你在 4 秒内获得完整的能量攻击，而不是 6 秒。
  • 过速装置更改：
    • 黄蜂轻甲
      • 过速装置现在根据战斗点的不同充电速度快了66%：每个战斗点0.99%而不是0.6%。
      • 干扰器状态效果由黄蜂轻甲的炸弹施加，持续6秒而不是3秒。
    • 十字军
      • 被动过速装置武器装载时间现在从50秒增加到70秒。
    • 独裁者
      • 效果半径从20米增加到25米。


7月9日（更新654）

  • 滑膛炮的«大口径短炮»装备改造不再增加炮弹重装时间；现在炮弹重装时间减少10%。

    • 球的闪电速度已重置为5米/秒，适用于所有修改。
    • 球的闪电射击延迟时间从0.5秒减少到0.3-0.2秒。

      • Mk6: 24.08 → 27.08;
      • Mk7: 24.82 → 27.82;
      • Mk7+: 26 → 29.
    • 连接第一个目标的射程降低了1米:
      • Mk1: 18 → 17;
      • Mk2: 19.18 → 18.18;
      • Mk3: 19.76 → 18.76;
      • Mk4: 20.35 → 19.35;
      • Mk5: 20.94 → 19.94;
      • Mk6: 21.38 → 20.38;
      • Mk7: 21.82 → 20.82;
      • Mk7+: 23 → 22。
  • «Mechanic» 无人机:
    • 支持队友获得的积分数量不再取决于受到影响的坦克数量；如果至少支持了1位队友，您将获得7分。
  • «突袭» 无人机:
    • 炮弹重装时间从12秒减少到3秒；
    • 道具炮弹重装时间的最大减少从 15 秒减少到 5 秒。
    • 道具炮弹重装时间的最小减少从3秒减少到1秒。
  • «驱动器» 无人机:
    • 炮弹重装时间从 15 秒减少到 5 秒;
    • 每次击杀过速装置炮弹重装时间的最大减少从30秒减少到了6秒。
    • 每次击杀所需的过速装置炮弹重装时间的最小减少从10秒减少到2秒。
  • «工程师» 无人机:
    • 炮弹重装时间从10秒减少到3秒；
  • «供应» 无人机:
    • 支持队友获得的积分数量不再取决于受到影响的坦克数量；如果至少支持了1位队友，您将获得5分。
  • «爆破手» 无人机:
    • 有效伤害半径内的伤害被减少了。无人机现在只会摧毁最近的对手，而不是所有在有效伤害半径内的对手。
  • 迷彩在 HD 底盘上的缩放被提高，以使迷彩在 SD 和 HD 皮肤上看起来相同。
  • 改进了游戏中的公告系统，现在你不会错过最重要的新闻。

    • 现在在没有看到目标 0.7 秒后，而不是 2 秒后保持瞄准。
  • 火箭炮:
    • 现在在未看到目标0.7秒后而不是1秒时保持瞄准。
  • 蜂王:
    • 应用穿甲状态效果的半径从1000米减少到50米。只有你可以看到的目标才会被施加此状态效果。

    • 反向加速度从15-20减少到9-14米/秒；
    • 重量从1300-2600减少到1000-2000。

    • 反向加速度从10-14减少到9-13米每秒；

    • Icicle的伤害从1500-3000 HP减少到1000-2000 HP。
  • 阿瑞斯:
    • 反向加速度从11-15减少到9-11米/秒；
    • 重量从1950-3900减少到1800-3600。
  • 独裁者:
    • 共享过速装置效果给队友所获得的战斗点数量不再取决于共享效果的队友数量。
    • 现在如果过速装置效果作用于至少1个队友（除了你的坦克），你将获得20点战斗积分。
    • 过速装置充电点现在在所有受影响的队友中平均分配，范围在过速装置射程内:
    • 恢复50%的过速装置变更点，而不是33%。
    • 这50%均匀分配给所有受影响的队友。

4月30日（更新645）

  • 五月假期 - 新任务和特殊活动已经在游戏中。
  • 将磁力炮的«吸血鬼纳米机器人»装备改造添加到超级礼盒。

  • 更新了道具和无人机的工作方式：
    • 将「Double 护甲」改名为「护甲提升」
    • 将「Double 伤害」改名为「伤害提升」
    • 默认情况下，这些道具的效果降低：
      • «护甲提升» decreases incoming 伤害 by 25%;
      • «伤害提升» 提高输出伤害 33%.
    • 如果一架装备无人机完全升级，«护甲提升»将把受到的伤害降低50%，而«伤害提升»将把输出的伤害提高100%，就像在此更新之前一样。
  • 更改了«布鲁特斯»无人机：
    • 它现在只增强道具，但不需要电池来工作。
  • 更改了«魔术师»无人机:
    • 现在它取代了之前的效果，增加了速度提升道具的效果，提升速度 10-30%；
    • 激活时使用 2 个额外的速度提升；
    • 炮弹重装时间已从10秒减少至3秒
  • 更改了«爆破手»无人机:
    • 现在它还将自毁时间减少了1秒。
  • 更改了默认音量的伤害声音:
    • 摧毁对手的声音现在更响亮；
    • 损坏的声音现在变得更安静了。
  • 修复了无法保存声音设置音量的漏洞。
  • 改进了战斗列表。
    • 您创建的战斗将在战斗列表中显示不同的颜色。
    • 当你打开一场战斗时，它在战斗列表中的颜色会有所不同。
    • 其他小改动

    • «电磁脉冲炮弹» 装备改造: 暴击伤害降低 30%，射击准备时间增加 20%，暴击伤害几率设定为 50%;

  • 滑膛炮:
    • 处理暴击伤害时，所有被碎片击中的目标都受到相同的暴击伤害；
    • «龙息» 装备改造仅在暴击伤害射击时应用着火状态效果。
  • 轰天炮:
    • 第一次修改的暴击伤害最高几率限制为20%，每次修改后增加至50%：
      • Mk1：20%；
      • Mk2：24%；
      • Mk3：28%；
      • Mk4: 31%;
      • Mk5: 35%;
      • Mk6: 39%;
      • Mk7: 43%;
      • Mk7+: 50%。
    • 在暴击射击中添加了一种新的暴击伤害类型，就像其他炮塔一样；
      • 装备改造：超累积炮弹、燃烧弹、冷冻炮弹、电磁脉冲炮弹和麻痹炮弹仅在暴击伤害的射击上生效状态效果。
  • 马格南:
    • «鱼叉导弹» 装备改造只有在直接命中时才能造成暴击伤害。
  • 火箭炮:
    • 暴击伤害是针对齐射中每个导弹单独计算的。
  • 激光炮:
    • 默认伤害现在射程从450（Mk1）提高到900（Mk7+）；
    • 增加了暴击伤害：800（Mk1）最高可达1600（Mk7+），具有固定50%的几率；
    • 当击中多个目标时，相同的暴击伤害会应用于所有目标；
    • «稳定轮环» 装备改造禁用暴击伤害，同时将默认伤害提高33%；
    • 「不稳定轮环」装备改造要么造成增加的暴击伤害 (+60%)，要么造成微不足道的默认伤害 - 100 HP：
    • «超空间炮弹» 装备改造不会造成暴击伤害.
    • «肾上腺素» 装备改造提高了默认伤害和暴击伤害。
  • 地雷:
    • 移除默认伤害射程;
    • 默认伤害更改为1500;
    • 增加1%的几率造成9999伤害。
  • «‎爆破手» 无人机:
    • 移除默认伤害射程;
    • 无法处理暴击伤害。
  • 添加了新的昂贵抗性防御模块，具有防护暴击伤害的能力:
    • Mk1: 可从超级礼盒获得;
    • Mk2: 15 000 水晶;
    • Mk3: 75 000 水晶;
    • Mk4: 150 000 水晶;
    • Mk5: 330 000 水晶;
    • Mk6: 500 000 水晶;
    • Mk7: 850 000 水晶;
    • Mk7+: 从 2,250,000 到 6,750,000 水晶，具体取决于你升级的速度。
  • 修复和更改用户界面。

  • 改变了制作十字军冰柱所需的时间。现在只需0.7秒，而之前是1.3秒！
  • 修复了游戏中以下元素的显示：‘首页’按钮，防护防御模块插槽，关于接收星级挑战等级奖励的通知等。

  • 修复了一个错误，该错误使坦克手在冷却期间可以取消装备防护防御模块。

    • 装备改造 «穿甲弹»: 暴击伤害减少25%.

  • Now when activating 十字军's 过速装置, an icicle appears near your 坦克's muzzle and start moving towards a target after a short delay
  • 修复了激光炮有时对阿瑞斯和十字军不造成伤害的bug。
  • 修复了阿瑞斯和十字军在激活过速装置时有时不射击的问题。
  • 马格南的鱼叉导弹装备改造的固定参数导致了极大的弹壳爆炸射程
  • 更改了主屏幕中的匹配小组界面

9月25日（更新621）

  • 所有底盘和炮塔的修改现在看起来都一样。
    • 我们已经开始更新游戏的界面和图形（HTML5界面，3D灌木，超高皮肤）。在未来世界中，我们将为每个炮塔和底盘逐个重制皮肤，使其更加现代化。依然只有一种默认皮肤，但它们会变得更好。为了做到这一点，我们不得不为所有炮塔和底盘选择一个修改皮肤进行重制，这就是M3（Mk7）修改皮肤。这是一个技术要求，也是实施计划的第一步。
  • 您现在可以通过点击HTML5右上角收到的通知来关闭它们。
  • 新增了一个通知，说明从超级礼盒中获取物品的几率增加了。
  • 添加了将军团标记显示到HTML5。
  • 添加了在聊天和大厅中显示 VIP 通行证版本的等级。
  • 修复了在您离开战斗后显示“返回到战斗”窗口的错误。
  • 修复了从幸运礼盒中获取后多次显示相同物品的错误。
  • 修复了当您已经激活 VIP 通行证时，幸运礼盒未显示 VIP 通行证作为可获得奖励的错误。
  • Fixed the bug that shows the sale badge for items which are not available for a 坦克手’s 等级.
  • 你现在可以购买 «Frost» 和 «Golden star» 迷彩，而不需要 VIP 通行证。
  • 修复了当一名坦克手从战斗进入大厅或车库，或反之时的内存泄漏。

    • «速度提升»（3）和«地雷»（4）道具现在从上士（6）等级开始在车库中可用。
    • The «Double Armour» (5) and «Double 伤害» (5) 道具 are now available in the 车库 starting from the 一级军士长 (9) 等级.
    • «电池» 道具 (6) 和 «布鲁特斯» 无人机 (6) 现在可以在车库中获取，从下士 (4) 等级开始。
    • The 匹配 system 允许 you to play only on 地图 that are unlocked for your 等级 now.
    • 里约地图上的光照变化。
    • «守卫者»无人机:
      • 效果持续时间从20秒减少到15秒；
      • 现在消耗2个更多的「双重护甲」道具；
      • 充电时间从20秒减少到3秒。
  • Changes in the HTML5 version:
    • 添加了对其他玩家过速装置状态的指示。
    • 修复了布局问题。

4月30日（更新600）

  • 变更列表:
    • The 普通幸运礼盒 has been replaced with a new one that contains 装备改造 for 炮塔 and 底盘.
    • 装备改造 for 炮塔 can no longer be bought from the 车库.
    • 改变了以下炮塔的装备改造特性：
      • 装备改造 for 冰风暴 «腐蚀混合物»:
        • 每秒伤害提升现在是10%，而不是5%.
      • 装备改造 for 磁力炮 «纳米反应器»:
        • Energy consumption decrease for 治疗模式 removed.
      • 装备改造 for 滑膛炮 «龙息»:
        • Clip 炮弹重装时间增加现在为 10%，而不是 15%。
      • 装备改造 for 滑膛炮 «高容量弹鼓»:
        • Clip 炮弹重装时间增加已被移除。
      • 装备改造 for 离子炮 «等离子体加速器»:
        • 炮弹重装时间 increase is now 20% instead of 25%.
      • 装备改造 for 离子炮 «重型等离子炮»:
        • Projectile 速度 decrease is now 35% instead of 50%.
      • 装备改造 for 火龙珠 «负场稳定»:
        • Shot 炮弹重装时间 increase is now 15% instead of 20%.
      • 装备改造 for 火龙珠 «等离子焰炬»:
        • 弹道速度降低现在是35%而不是50%。
      • 装备改造 for 火龙珠 «狂暴»:
        • Energy used per shot increase is now 20% instead of 30%.
      • 装备改造 for 轰天炮 «自动加农炮»:
        • 最低 and 最高伤害 decrease is now 75% instead of 80%.
      • 装备改造 for 火箭炮 «Missile launcher "猎人中甲"»:
        • 增加了100%的投射物速度提升;
        • Removed 最高 projectile 速度 limit.
      • 装备改造 for 火箭炮 «Missile launcher "旋风"»:
        • 瞄准时间增加现在是25%，而不是30%.
      • 装备改造 for 火箭炮 «Missile launcher “轴”»：
        • 炮弹重装时间 increase is now 15% instead of 20%
      • 装备改造 for 雷暴炮 «穿甲弹药»:
        • 射击率增加了10%。
      • 装备改造 for 雷暴炮 «“大锤" rounds»:
        • Projectile 速度 decrease is now 50% instead of 60%.
      • 装备改造 for 激光炮 «更快速的水平跟踪»:
        • Vertical autoaim decrease is now 20% instead of 30%.
      • 装备改造 for 激光炮 «Electromagnetic accelerator "侦察机"»:
        • 最高伤害降低现在是30%而不是40%。
      • 装备改造 for 激光炮 «大口径弹药»:
        • 炮弹重装时间 increase removed.
      • 装备改造 for 马格南 «自动火药装载机»:
        • 炮弹重装时间的增加现在为10%而不是20%.
      • 装备改造 for 镭射炮 «重型电容器»:
        • 水平瞄准速度降低已移除。
      • 装备改造 for 镭射炮 «轻型电容器»: 使武器系统更具有效能。
        • 水平瞄准速度现在为100%而不是30%.

      • Loading into 战斗 is now faster.

4月24日（更新599）

  • 变更列表:
    • 发布了8个底盘修改用于猎人中甲。
    • 现在，防护防御模块不再减少冷冻（减速）和着火（后燃）效果。
    • 剑圣 has 50% 抗性 from 冷冻 (slow-down) 速度 and 着火 (after-burn) 伤害.
    • 泰坦’s and 黄蜂轻甲’s 过速装置:
      • 泰坦’s dome no longer protects from 冷冻 (slow-down) and 着火 (after-burn) effects but still decreases heating 伤害;
      • 当你放置圆顶时，除了禁用其他圆顶，它还会禁用黄蜂轻甲的过速装置中的炸弹。
    • 猎人中甲’s 过速装置:
      • 眩晕持续时间从2.7秒增加到3秒；
      • 道具禁用持续时间从3秒增加到5秒。
  • HTML5 中的更改列表:
    • Triple buffering is now controlled by the 玩家’s browser. Unnecessary framebuffer switches are no longer loaded while rendering, so 图形 productivity was increased.
    • Added a confirmation window for deleting a 好友 from 好友 list.
    • Added some translations.
    • 修正了战斗聊天中的汉字可读性。

      • The dome no longer repairs 坦克, but instead increases 护甲;

      • Decreased round 速度 from 250 m/s to 225 m/s;
      • Decreased average blast 半径 from 5 meters to 4 meters;

  • 过速装置的变化:
    • 猛犸象的过速装置:
      • Removed invincibility;
      • 忽视物理影响被删除；

      • 速度提升从30%增加到40%;
      • Added instant repair;
      • Added instant removal of 冷冻 and 着火 effects;
      • Cannot be disabled by 黄蜂轻甲's 过速装置.
    • 猎人中甲's 过速装置:
      • Decreased effect 半径 from 30 to 25 meters;
      • Decreased 持续时间 time from 3 to 2.7 seconds;

    • 极速炮的修改 «更快速的水平跟踪»:

      • now reduces slowdown in 炮塔 rotation by 50%, from 70%.
    • 雷暴炮 alteration «穿甲弹药»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • additionally increase strength of impact and 后坐力 by 10%.
    • 激光炮改动 «更快速的水平跟踪»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • now increases 转向灵活度 by 40%, from 35%.
    • 激光炮 alteration «稳定轮环»:
      • price reduced fromо 100,000 to 35,000;
      • additionally retains 启动加速度 of the shot through targets by 100%.
    • 激光炮 alteration «大口径弹药»:
      • 此外，延迟时间在射击前增加20%。
    • 镭射炮 alteration «重型电容器»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • 现在将最小伤害提高20%，从25%增加。
      • now increases 炮弹重装时间 by 25%, from 20%.
  • Option to rent alterations removed from the game.
  • Gameplay alterations are now unlocked according to 等级, not 炮塔 modifications.
  • Now only one gameplay alteration can be 装备 for each 炮塔.
  • 现在炮塔射击的标准颜色不再依赖于其修改。


October 30 (Update 532)

  • 任务 system reworked:
    • 任务 chains replaced with 每周任务.
    • Added new 幸运礼盒 type — 每周任务礼盒.
      • 每周任务礼盒 includes a set of bonuses: 水晶 and 道具.
      • 每周任务礼盒只能作为完成每周任务的奖励获得。
    • Added new types of 每日任务:
      • activate 过速装置 in 战斗;
      • finish 战斗;
      • finish 战斗 in specific 模式.
    • 3x hours of vip as a 任务奖励 was removed from the game.
    • “Collect 道具” 任务 can now be completed by activating specific 道具.
    • Slightly increased the cost of changing 每日任务.
  • 9 new 无人机 added for purchase in the 车库.
  • 3 new 无人机套件 added to the 商店:
    • «Trinity» — «供应», «守卫者», «奔跑者» 无人机;
    • «无人机 amid a clear sky» — «魔术师», «助推器», «救生员» 无人机;
    • «Full house» — «破坏者», «露营者», «爆破手» 无人机.
  • In the «Second coming» 套件 the «供应» 无人机 was replaced with the new «工兵» 无人机.
  • Changes to 无人机 balance:
    • 突袭:
      • changed bonus for the 持续时间 of active 道具:
        • with no 升级: (7 → 3), sec.
      • recharge increased from 10 to 12 seconds.
    • 驱动器:
      • changed the amount of time for 过速装置 recharge that is reduced for each enemy 坦克 destroyed::
        • fully upgraded: (20 → 30), sec/kill.
      • recharge reduced from 15 to 12 seconds.
    • 工程师:
      • recharge increased from 5 to 10 seconds.
    • 供应:
      • now available for purchase from the 上尉等级, instead of WO5;
      • price increased from 50,000 to 90,000 水晶.


October 19 (Update 530)

July 12 (Update 469)

  • New feature - “过速装置” added to the game.
    • This 过速装置 activates all 5 道具 (except 金箱子) for you and your teammates nearby;
    • “过速装置 ON/OFF” option added to 专家战场设置;
    • 过速装置 is turned off by default in 格式战斗, except 跑酷.
  • Changes to 维修工具 mechanic:
    • Initially 维修工具 instantly restores 1000 HP and reduces 着火 and 冷冻 effects, and then additionally restores 3000 hit points over 3 seconds;
    • The repair-over-time effect will be interrupted if any 伤害 is sustained;
    • 一旦坦克完全修复，修复效果将被中断。
  • Changes to 道具 active/冷却 times:
    • 维修工具
      • 持续时间: 3 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • Double 护甲
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • Double 伤害
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 速度提升
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 地雷
      • 伤害: Unchanged
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
  • Changes to destroyed 坦克 disappearing delay and respawn times:
    • Destroyed 坦克 disappearing delay time reduced from 3.5 sec to 1.5 sec
    • Respawn delay time increased from 2 sec to 4 sec

    • New 迷彩 applies only after next respawn.

March 29 (Update 451)

  • Changes to microupgrades:
    • Number of steps for M2 底盘, 炮塔 and 防御模块 decreased to 10;
    • Number of steps for M3 底盘 and 炮塔 decreased to 20 (steps for 防御模块 remain 15);
    • Total step cost for M2 底盘, 炮塔 and 防御模块 decreased and now equals to the cost of the stock M3 modification of the item;
    • Total step cost for M3 底盘, 炮塔 and 防御模块 remains the same.
  • Changes to 每日任务:
    • Now 每日任务 objectives can be only completed in standard (non-PRO) 战斗;
    • 奖励 for 每日任务 increased by 10%.
  • Changes to Auto-completion system:
    • 监控启动延迟现在为60秒（原为3分钟）；
    • Auto-completion waiting time is now 15 sec (was 30 sec);
    • 冷却 after cancelling auto-completion is now 10 sec (was 25 sec).
  • 等级 limits when creating a 战斗 expanded for all 等级.
  • Some bugs with 马格南 fixed.
  • 暴击 errors disabled:
    • Up until now, when the 3D坦克 client received a “strange” instruction, it would spit out a 暴击 Error and throw you out of the game. With this update, we’ll be disabling the 暴击 Error (when bugs will go off you will not be disconnected from the 服务器).

September 22

    • simplified 控制;
    • added possibility to 射击 without using 辽源;

    • removed black filling in 辽源模式;
    • visually enhanced the 辽源;

    • added new 地图公路大战 from MonkeyMagic.

  • 密码 length was limited to 32 symbols.


September 1

  • Payments for 水晶 using Paypal have resumed.
  • The cost of all payments through SMS are now include VAT.
  • The 最低 payment through SMS payment for MTC subscribers has been set at 300 roubles. This change was made by the service provider itself. In the past an error could be experienced when attempting to make a payment less than 300 roubles.
  • The ability to make a one symbol 密码 without an 电子邮件 has been excluded.


August 25

  • The registration form has been improved. It has become smaller, more convenient — nicer.

  • In the loading screen «TV grid» has been replaced with the game logo.

  • We have simplified the game entering mechanics. Now after clicking the Start

button a newcomer enters the 战斗 without registration. There he can meet 坦克手们 of 新兵, 二等兵 and 一等兵等级. Such a 玩家 automatically gets the 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, where NNNNN is unique number.

  • A 玩家 is offered to fill the registration form only after

reaching 二等兵等级.

  • If you are not a newcomer, but also found yourself in a 战斗 with newbies and with 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, then click «I have an 账号» button in the upper part of the game menu. We have created a basic achievement system, which 帮助 newcomers to learn some basic elements of the game. Now you get 水晶 prizes for such actions, as registration after the first 战斗, joining the first 战斗 after registration, first buying in the 车库 etc.
  • We have changed loading indications. Now it looks like the charging

mechanism of artillery gun. Also game advices are shown during loading.

  • We have simplified the registration form.
  • The Tab button now is functional in all fields.
  • You need to enter less information to register. Only 昵称 and

密码 are required.

  • The Hall of Fame button was removed from the game menu.
  • Every 玩家 now can create a no-道具战斗 without a 通行证. The

创建者 also can enter this 战斗 without a 通行证.

  • 我们已经改进了 WebMoney 付款选项。现在您可以选择

currency and amount of 水晶 right in the payment section.

optimized.

button.

  • The sum on the Add button in the 车库 is adjusted for Double

水晶.

  • Notification about an active Double 水晶 bonus card is shown in

the payment section.

  • The PayPal button is temporary removed from the payment section. We’ll start to

take PayPal payments again soon.

  • Now you can’t skip the nick checking procedure.
  • The respawn was fixed in the blue 团队 on 山顶城堡地图.
  • The wall bug was fixed on 辽源地图.
  • The 迷彩 «Champion» (for 军团 Tournament winners) and Acid (for TOF

winners) were given 防护 against the 镭射炮.

the bridge.

March 21

  • We have realized sources storage in local SharedObject of Flash 玩家. It 允许 us to abandon browser caching system, which is not very reliable. For example, sources could disappear from browser cache because of its limited 大小. Now sources are downloaded from the 服务器 only if they were changed. It can drastically reduce time of game loading.

February 3

  • One of the errors causing the appearance of so-called «invisibles» has been eliminated
  • All New Year’s decorations including, Christmas trees (which had replaced 旗子), holiday parachutes, wrapped presents, and holiday-themed billboards have been removed.

  • The shopping cart icon used for entering payment section has been replaced with a «购买» button.
  • The 车库 has been optimized through the use of progressive loading. Upon entering the 车库 only visible items are loaded, allowing for faster entry. All 其他 information will be loaded when 玩家 scroll through item lists.
  • We have launched a notification system that notifies 玩家 the moment they achieve a new 等级. The message is displayed during 战斗.
  • We have also launched an alert system, informing 玩家 about new items available for purchase in the 车库. A message displaying the icons of these items will appear when a 玩家 receives a new 等级 and leaves 战斗 or enters the game. Click on the icon guides to the description of the item in the 车库.

  • Overloaded database, caused game instability, was modified. Now all 玩家’s achievements are not only saved but also stored through Redis. This solves a lot of issues. Due to this update search logic in the Hall of Fame is temporarily changed. To find user, you should type his full 昵称, not part of it.

If it wasn’t, tech support 团队 automatically gets task and 玩家 receives a letter about that. Note: if 玩家 made a few identical payments, it is necessary to specify that in payment bug 报告 form.

  • Time checking system for resource loading was added. If resources can not be loaded for certain time the loading will be started from the beginning.

July 8

  • There are two new guns: 冰风暴 and 火龙珠.
  • Each 底盘 now has its own 重量.
  • Links for the 战斗 in 聊天 channel are clickable now. When you click the link you see the list of 战斗 and information about them.
  • There are new 地图: 农场 and 山顶城堡 from Nobius; 平原 and 延迟 Pong from A_Creature; 天空管道 (idea from JlEHb) and 火车站2 from Flanagun.
  • We’ve changed 旗子 indication in 战斗. Written messages from the center of the screen were taken away. Now all informative symbols are allocated in the bottom right corner.
  • Different modifications of 蜂王, 维京 and 猛犸象 have different appearance now.
  • In the Hall of Fame we’ve improved search system based on 玩家’s 昵称. Now a few letters from the nick in the search line disappear if there are not any similarities with search request.
  • All links in the 聊天 channel are clickable now but when you are trying to proceed the link which is not marked as trusted you get warning.
  • We have made 服务器 optimization to reduce the amount of lags.
  • We have changed terminology. The word «Kill» was replaced by «Destroy», «Died» by «Lost», «Suicided» by «Selfdestructed».
  • 在注册过程中没有指定电子邮件时，电子邮件变化的问题得到了解决。
  • 离子炮 charges geometry was experimentally reduced. These charges don’t cling to objects now.
  • 电子邮件 in the 聊天 channel now look like links. Click to the link automatically launches your default 电子邮件 client.
  • We’ve launched bad 语言 checking system for names of 战斗.
  • Evacuation system was improved. 战斗 migrate to 其他服务器 gradually not overloading receiving 服务器 with great amount of 玩家 at a time.
  • 蜂王 M1 底盘 price cut to 1350 水晶.


June 4

  • New 礼物 system. Now you can find one of three different presents in the 每日 bonus. It can be 道具 (1 or 2), 水晶 or one day no-道具战斗通行证. 玩家 get the 礼物 starting from the third 等级 only.
  • We took away buttons PayPal (temporarily), LiqPay (temporarily), EasyPay and RBK Money from payment section.
  • We added Prepaid Cards subsection in the payment section. Payments through Wallie, Paysafecard, Rixty and CashU are now supported.
  • Banned 玩家 now gets information about the period of his ban right in the 聊天. Nobody beside him can see this message.
  • From now on the 聊天 is open for 玩家 with the 二等兵 and higher 等级.
  • We have solved the problem with invisible 坦克.
  • There are drop points for golden crates in every 地图 now.
  • Different 独裁者 modifications have different appearances now.
  • Each 磁力炮 modification got its own shooting effect color.
  • The problem with 电子邮件 confirmation has been successfully resolved.
  • We launched the second part of the 账号防护 system. If you specified an 电子邮件 in your 账号 you will see the button «Change 电子邮件 and 密码» instead of standard form for 电子邮件 and 密码 changing. When you click this button you get the 电子邮件 with the link forwarding you to the page with the form for 电子邮件 and 密码 changing. If you didn’t specify an 电子邮件 you can make changes right in the 设置 menu without confirmation.
  • Now you can enter no-道具战斗 for one-time payment in the amount of 50 水晶.
  • One month no-道具战斗通行证 price cut. Now it costs 500 水晶 only.
  • There are new 地图: 2042 by GT-Razer, 小岛 by Figishe, 孔贝 by Figishe, 沙漠 by Figishe, 铁塔 by M0ONL1ght, 通行证 by Figishe, 甲板9号 by M0ONL1ght, 峡谷 by M0ONL1ght, 多边形 by Figishe and Plato by Figishe.


May 21

  • Now a nick is checked against prohibited words during registration;
  • Public command #feedback added — it is a switch to the system of ideas and suggestions feedback.tankionline.com;
  • Hash is changed with 密码 change now;
  • Anti-foul 语言 system doesn’t ban users anymore. It replaces forbidden words to symbols *** now;
  • New system of evacuation implemented: now the 战斗 will switch to another 服务器 with all the 玩家 in it during restart;
  • Changed one of alternative buttons — (similar to Del), now Ctrl+ is the analog of Del;
  • Candidate moderators can give 5-minute bans now.


May 8

  • Fixed a bug in the 3D engine, which led to a 暴击 error in the 战斗.


五月一日

  • 声音 of shot of 雷暴炮 is 30% quieter now.
  • 声音 of shot of 离子炮 is 20% quieter now.
  • There is no ban for links to 战斗 containing single letter many times (like fffffffffffff).

  • 猛犸象 — a new armour available.
  • A limit for 玩家 amount on 动感区域 — 12 玩家.

April 23

  • 雷暴炮 — a new weapon is available.
  • 维京 — a new armour is available.
  • 二等兵战斗 link problem has been fixed
  • 轰天炮、黄蜂轻甲和磁力炮的不同外观
  • Different effect of shots for grades of 轰天炮
  • 磁力炮的新优先事项。治疗受伤队友为最高优先级，对敌人的优先级为中等，对「健康」的队友为最低优先级。
  • Alternative keys for some actions: Del, PgUp ], PgDown [.
  • New 聊天 command available for all 玩家 #updates — link to «Patch Notes / Updates».
  • New 地图: Промзона/工厂之战 by GT-Razer, Зона / 动感区域 by M0ONL1ght, Тишина / 寂静 by Figishe
  • All 玩家 will be moved to another 服务器 when restart is launched.
  • 持续时间 of banning generated by bot is reduced to day.
  • 轻微修改盔甲规格（黄蜂轻甲 М2，猎人中甲 М1，猎人中甲 М2，泰坦 М3，独裁者 М1）。
  • 轰天炮M2规格的细微变化。
  • 泰坦 М3 costs 900 水晶 now.


April 1

  • Second stage of 服务器 optimization has been finished. Lags were greatly reduced. Lags are network latencies during which 坦克 switch 职务, bonuses and 旗子 are taken with delay.
  • Purchase or improvement requires confirmation now.
  • Order #等级 renamed into #等级.
  • Added public order #论坛 — switch to 论坛.
  • Fixed bugs with 密码 and 电子邮件 change in 设置.
  • Now bonus 水晶 for invited 好友 can be viewed on «Invitation 统计数据» button.
  • Fixed bug with 水晶 receiving for invited 好友. They will be accounted today.


March 30

  • First stage of 服务器 optimization has been finished. Lags should reduce. Lags are network latencies during which 坦克 switch 职务, bonuses and 旗子 are taken with delay.


March 19

  • Now the distance between a 旗子 carrier and the base is taken into 账号 during 水晶 calculation for 旗子 return in 互夺军旗.
  • Now bug 报告 can be sent by testers only. If you have a problem with payment, fill in the form and send a message from payment section. All 其他 problems and questions are discussed at 论坛.
  • Now 火焰炮 and 猎人中甲 modifications look differently.
  • 现在火焰炮的改动使得火焰的颜色不同。
  • Coats were rebalanced (Swamp + 2% from 离子炮 (total 15%); Safari + 5% from 轰天炮; Dragon + 5% from 磁力炮; Roger + 5% from 激光炮; Jaguar — 10% from 火焰炮, но +5% from 激光炮 and +5% from 磁力炮; Electra +5% from 激光炮).
  • Added new 地图 with new props 炼油厂保卫战.
  • 地图 which used to be available to 低等级 are now available for higher ones also: 训练场 II, 演练场 II and 小桥之战 II.
  • 新订单出现了 (#等级 — 切换到论坛主题 «等级», #军团 — 切换到论坛线程 «军团»).


March 10

  • Experimentally reduced points for 磁力炮 cure. Coefficient was reduced from 2 to 1,5. Experiment will last for a week.


March 5

  • Button «Improve» is placed next to «Set» in the 车库.
  • Every modification of 炮塔 and shells is described now in a 特殊 table which is placed in the 车库.
  • Fixed bugs in 火焰炮 and 磁力炮: 火焰炮 had greater 伤害 effect than it had to, 磁力炮 had less 伤害 effect than it had to. Now similar modifications of 火焰炮 and 磁力炮 have equal 伤害 effect in full charge.
  • Fixed bug when 火焰炮 effect during 射击 while moving was displayed incorrectly. There used to be very long flame while moving backwards and very short one — while moving forward.
  • Abolished 通行证 — Double 分数. All the 玩家 who purchased the 通行证 during making changes on 服务器 will get their 水晶 back.
  • A new 通行证 was added — 分数 multiplier 通行证: multiplies all received points by 25%, lifetime — one month.
  • A new 通行证 was added — No-道具战斗: enables you to create and enter no-道具战斗, lifetime — one month.
  • 激光炮和离子炮的改动现在看起来不同了。
  • 现在地雷被纳入日常礼物中。


February 10

  • Added new consumable — 地雷. View details in FAQ.
  • Done effects visualization. View details in FAQ.
  • 使用后改变了消耗品阻挡时间的可视化（冷却）.
  • Improved automatic anti-foul 语言 system: now the 聊天 knows 1 300 000 Russian words. If you do not misspell the words, false responses will be 珍奇.
  • Improved registration form — added check-up of nick availability (after you enter the needed nick and are inactive in entry field for two seconds or switching to 密码 entry field, the nick is checked and next to it you see a tick or a red 十字路口).
  • Now you get twice as much points for curing the 坦克手 who carries a 旗子.
  • Summer is back! All the 地图 now have pleasant green landscape.
  • 地图黑色城堡 and 城堡争夺 are back.
  • Added new 地图核电站 from Duke 2.0
  • Lessened 大厅 loading time due to reduction of loaded 地图 preview, now they load when needed.
  • Now every modification of 轰天炮, 火焰炮, 离子炮 and 激光炮 has own 图形 effect.
  • 现在您可以在支付部分使用备用支付系统进行VISA/MasterCard支付。
  • Solved bug when points were not accounted when you kill 磁力炮 owner or a patient during cure.


January 22

  • Finally accepted modification of 离子炮: 垂直角度 of 瞄准 increased greatly (two degrees up, one down), lowered 速度 of bullets, finally accepted 伤害
  • 引入了没有消耗品的付费战斗。
  • Fixed bug when a consumable timer is stopped up after getting bonus.
  • Karma was introduced in 聊天: if you misbehaved, the 聊天 remembers it and takes into 账号 when giving automatic ban, but soon forgets about misbehaviour.
  • All newcomers will appear in the 战斗 at once without entering game menu.
  • 现在你可以通过电子邮件邀请好友参加游戏。
  • Payment systems Yandex. Dengi and Webmoney were moved to another payment aggregator (2Pay). But you still can pay through the former aggregator (OnlineDengi).
  • Now if you, for some 原因, lost connection with the game (being in the 战斗), you can return without loosing your achievements. Time to return into the 战斗 — 2 minutes.
  • Changed algorithm of anti-foul 语言 system. Within some period of time there can be false responses, since we’re perfecting the system. If you have examples of false responses please send them to 帮助@tankionline.com
  • Changed algorithm of anti-flood system, now anti-flood 关注 typing of similar symbols in a row in one message.
  • 旗子 finally have taken their stand.
  • Fixed bug of mismatch between number of 玩家 in the 战斗 list and 战场信息 (9/11).
  • Changed the 声音 of 离子炮 shooting.


January 16

  • Experimental changes in the 离子炮 gun: the 垂直角度 for automatic targeting is now increased (3 degrees upwards, 3 downwards), 速度 of flight of the individual shells is lowered.


1月14日

  • Eliminated a vulnerability that allowed to increase the 速度 in 战斗 (aka 速度 hack). Now if you somehow 速度 up the 坦克, you’ll be automatically kicked from the 战斗.


January 12

  • 离子炮 is experimentally strengthened for one week. You can discuss the current 统计 and post your impressions/suggestions here
  • The referral banned display problem is now solved.

August 7

  • Added 聊天 orders to 禁止 messages from users:
    • /禁止 name – 禁止 messages from the 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /unblock name – resume messages from 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /blocklist – view the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).
    • /unblockall – clear the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).

The list of blocked users is kept in Shared Objects, so if you enter the game from the 其他 computer – it won't work.
